msg:The location of the hotel is in Qianjiang New City. Although it is not in the C position, it is right on the riverside. Crossing the road is the flood embankment. The river view room has a good view, you can see the bridge, it is very convenient to go for a walk or run by the river in the evening.
The hotel facilities exceeded my expectations. The restaurants and breakfast varieties are good. Dining at the high-altitude river view restaurant is also refreshing. The hotel is equipped with a gym and a heated swimming pool, which is great for those who need to keep exercising during business trips, and it is also worthy of the 5-star standard. At the same time, the room is equipped with a bathtub, which is also convenient for relaxation.
The fly in the oin**ent is that the hotel is slightly out of the way, and it takes about 10 minutes by taxi to get to Vientiane City. In addition, this hotel seems to have a large number of reception groups, and the people living in it are mixed and slightly noisy. It is also because of this reason that the bathtub in the room is not dared to use. At the same time, the overall service level of the front desk reception of the hotel is a bit weak. When I arrived at the store at noon, I was told directly that there was no room, and then I sent it to the concierge depar**ent. There was no guidance, and I also said that I could not register for check-in information first. This is the first time I encountered this in a five-star hotel. I noticed that there was no phone call after the hotel room was vacated, which affected the arrangement a bit. This kind of soft service needs to be improved!
Of course, the price-performance ratio of more than 500 yuan per night is still relatively high. It is a high-end hotel with high cost performance, but it cannot be called five-star luxury. It is recommended for those with limited budget in the Qianjiang New City area!
